<p>Experience.Awards</p>
<p><b>  Award </b></p>
<p><b>Situation</b></p>
<p> </p>
<p>1 </p>
<p>The group accomplished little or had </p>
<p>a very short session.</p>
<p> </p>
<p>2 </p>
<p>The group had more successes than </p>
<p>failures.</p>
<p> </p>
<p>3 </p>
<p>The group succeeded greatly, and their </p>
<p>adventure had a significant impact on </p>
<p>the overall story.</p>
<p>Social.Conflict.Results</p>
<p> <b>Margin of Victory </b></p>
<p><b>Result</b></p>
<p> </p>
<p>Tie </p>
<p>The issue is unsettled and no action is </p>
<p>taken until new and more compelling </p>
<p>evidence can be presented to reopen </p>
<p>the  negotiation.  In  a  court  case,  the </p>
<p>defense  would  win  as  the  burden  of </p>
<p>proof is on the prosecution.</p>
<p> </p>
<p>1-2 </p>
<p>The  target  isn’t  truly  convinced  but </p>
<p>decides it’s better to be safe than sorry. </p>
<p>He  provides  the  minimum  amount  of </p>
<p>support possible. In a court case, the </p>
<p>jury  barely  finds  reasonable  doubt  if </p>
<p>the defense wins, or assigns minimal </p>
<p>sentencing if the prosecution wins.</p>
<p> </p>
<p>3-4 </p>
<p>The target is reasonably convinced. He </p>
<p>grants  the  help  requested,  more  or </p>
<p>less, but may have conditions or ask </p>
<p>favors  in  return.  In  a  court  case,  the </p>
<p>judge invokes severe sentencing if the </p>
<p>prosecution wins. If the defense wins </p>
<p>the defendant is cleared of all charges.</p>
<p> </p>
<p>5+ </p>
<p>The  target  is  sure  of  his  decision.  He </p>
<p>provides more support than requested. </p>
<p>If the prosecution wins in a court case, </p>
<p>the defendant receives the maximum </p>
<p>penalty.</p>

<h1 style="page-break-before:always; "></h1>
<p>--Page--186</p>
<p>Savage.Worlds</p>
<p>Fright.Table</p>
<p><b>  1d20* </b></p>
<p><b>Effect</b></p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>1-4 </b></p>
<p><b>Adrenaline Surge:</b> The hero’s “fight” </p>
<p>response takes over. He adds +2 to </p>
<p>all Trait and damage rolls on his next </p>
<p>action.</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>5-8 </b></p>
<p><b>Shaken: </b>The character is Shaken.</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>9-12 </b></p>
<p><b>Panicked:</b> The character immediately </p>
<p>moves his full Pace plus running die </p>
<p>away from the danger and is Shaken.</p>
<p><b>  13-16 </b></p>
<p><b>Minor  Phobia: </b> The  character  gains </p>
<p>a Minor Phobia Hindrance somehow </p>
<p>associated with the trauma.</p>
<p><b>  17-18 </b></p>
<p><b>Major Phobia: </b>The character gains a </p>
<p>Major Phobia Hindrance.</p>
<p><b>  19-20 </b></p>
<p><b>The Mark of Fear: </b>The hero is Shaken </p>
<p>and  also  suffers  some  cosmetic </p>
<p>physical  alteration—a  white  streak </p>
<p>forms  in  the  hero’s  hair,  his  eyes </p>
<p>twitch constantly, or some other minor </p>
<p>physical alteration. This reduces his </p>
<p>Charisma by 1.</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>21+ </b></p>
<p><b>Heart  Attack:</b>  The  hero  is  so </p>
<p>overwhelmed with fear that his heart </p>
<p>stutters. He  becomes Incapacitated </p>
<p>and must make a Vigor roll at –2. If </p>
<p>successful,  he’s  Shaken  and  can’t </p>
<p>attempt  to  recover  for  1d4  rounds. </p>
<p>If he fails, he dies in 2d6 rounds. A </p>
<p>Healing roll at –4 saves the victim’s </p>
<p>life, but he remains Incapacitated.</p>
<p>Injury.Table</p>
<p> <b> 2d6 </b></p>
<p><b>Wound</b></p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>2 </b></p>
<p><b>Unmentionables: </b>If the injury is </p>
<p>permanent, reproduction is out of the </p>
<p>question without miracle surgery or </p>
<p>magic. There is no other effect from </p>
<p>this result.</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>3-4 </b></p>
<p><b>Arm:</b> Roll left or right arm randomly; it’s </p>
<p>unusable like the One Arm Hindrance </p>
<p>(though if the primary arm is affected, </p>
<p>off-hand penalties still apply to the </p>
<p>other).</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>5-9 </b></p>
<p><b>Guts:</b> Your hero catches one </p>
<p>somewhere between the crotch and </p>
<p>the chin. Roll 1d6: </p>
<p><i> </i></p>
<p><i> </i></p>
<p><i> 1-2 </i></p>
<p><i>Broken:</i> Agility reduced a die </p>
<p>type (minimum d4).</p>
<p><i> </i></p>
<p><i> </i></p>
<p><i> 3-4 </i></p>
<p><i>Battered:</i> Vigor reduced a die </p>
<p>type (minimum d4).</p>
<p><i> </i></p>
<p><i> </i></p>
<p><i> 5-6 </i></p>
<p><i>Busted:</i> Strength reduced a die </p>
<p>type (minimum d4).</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>10 </b></p>
<p><b>Leg:</b> Gain the Lame Hindrance (or the </p>
<p>One Leg Hindrance if already Lame).</p>
<p><b> 11-12 </b></p>
<p><b>Head:</b> A grievous injury to the head. </p>
<p>Roll 1d6: </p>
<p><i> </i></p>
<p><i> </i></p>
<p><i>  1-2 </i></p>
<p><i>Hideous Scar: </i>Your hero now </p>
<p>has the Ugly Hindrance.</p>
<p> </p>
<p> </p>
<p>  <i>3-4 </i></p>
<p><i>Blinded:</i> An eye is damaged. </p>
<p>Gain the One Eye Hindrance (or the </p>
<p>Blind Hindrance if he only had one </p>
<p>good eye).</p>
<p> </p>
<p> </p>
<p> <i> 5-6 </i></p>
<p><i>Brain Damage:</i> Massive trauma </p>
<p>to the head. Smarts reduced one die </p>
<p>type (min d4).</p>
<h1 style="page-break-before:always; "></h1>
<p>--Page--187</p>
<p>Reference</p>
<p>Out.of.Control</p>
<p> </p>
<p><b>2d6 </b></p>
<p><b>Effect</b></p>
<p> </p>
<p><b>2</b> </p>
<p><b>Roll Over:</b> The vehicle performs a Slip and rolls over 1d6 times in that direction. Roll </p>
<p>collision damage for the vehicle and everyone inside. Any exterior-mounted weapons </p>
<p>or accessories are ruined.</p>
<p> </p>
<p><b>3–4</b> </p>
<p><b>Spin:</b> Move the vehicle 1d6” in the direction of the maneuver, or 1d6” away from a damaging </p>
<p>blow. Roll a d12, read it like a clock facing, and point the vehicle in that direction. </p>
<p> </p>
<p><b>5-9</b> </p>
<p><b>Skid:</b> Move the vehicle 1d4” left or right (in the direction of a failed maneuver, or away </p>
<p>from a damaging attack).</p>
<p> <b> 10–11</b> </p>
<p><b>Slip:</b> Move the vehicle 1d6” left or right (in the direction of a failed maneuver, or away from </p>
<p>a damaging attack).</p>
<p> </p>
<p><b>12</b> </p>
<p><b>Flip: </b>The vehicle flips end over end 1d4 times. Move it forward that many increments of </p>
<p>its own length. Roll collision damage for the vehicle, its passengers, and anything it hits. </p>
<p>Slow and heavy vehicles such as tanks (GM’s discretion) don’t flip but suffer a Slip or </p>
<p>Skid instead.</p>
<p>Critical.Hits</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>2d6 </b></p>
<p><b>Effect</b></p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>2</b> </p>
<p><b>Scratch and Dent:</b> The attack merely scratches the paint. There’s no permanent damage.</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>3</b> </p>
<p><b>Engine:</b> The engine is hit. Oil leaks, pistons misfire, etc. Acceleration is halved (round </p>
<p>down). This does not affect deceleration, however.</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>4</b> </p>
<p><b>Locomotion:</b> The wheels, tracks, or whatever have been hit. Halve the vehicle’s Top Speed </p>
<p>immediately. If the vehicle is pulled by animals, the shot hits one of them instead.</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>5</b> </p>
<p><b>Controls:</b> The control system is hit. Until a Repair roll is made, the vehicle can only perform </p>
<p>turns to one side (1–3 left, 4–6 right). This may prohibit certain maneuvers as well.</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>6–8</b> </p>
<p><b>Chassis:</b> The vehicle suffers a hit in the body with no special effects.</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>9–10</b> </p>
<p><b>Crew:</b> A random crew member is hit. The damage from the attack is rerolled. If the character </p>
<p>is inside the vehicle, subtract the vehicle’s Armor from the damage. Damage caused by </p>
<p>an explosion affects all passengers in the vehicle.</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>11</b> </p>
<p><b>Weapon:</b> A random weapon on the side of the vehicle that was hit is destroyed and may </p>
<p>no longer be used. If there is no weapon, this is a Chassis hit instead.</p>
<p><b> </b></p>
<p><b>12</b> </p>
<p><b>Wrecked:</b> The vehicle is wrecked and automatically goes Out of Control.</p>
